SELECT [t].[Id], [t].[Capacity], [t].[CountryCount], [t].[CreatedDate], [t].[Desc], [t].[Duration], [t].[EndDate], [t].[Image], [t].[Name], [t].[OldPrice], [t].[Price], [t].[StartDate], [t0].[Id], [t0].[CityId], [t0].[CreatedDate], [t0].[TourId], [t0].[Id0], [t0].[CountryId], [t0].[CreatedDate0], [t0].[Name], [t0].[Id1], [t0].[CreatedDate1], [t0].[Name0], [t2].[Id], [t2].[ActivityId], [t2].[CreatedDate], [t2].[TourId], [t2].[Id0], [t2].[CreatedDate0], [t2].[Name], [t4].[Id], [t4].[AmenityId], [t4].[CreatedDate], [t4].[TourId], [t4].[Id0], [t4].[CreatedDate0], [t4].[Name], [e].[Id], [e].[CreatedDate], [e].[Name], [e].[TourId], [p].[Id], [p].[CreatedDate], [p].[Day], [p].[Description], [p].[Title], [p].[TourId]
FROM [Tours] AS [t]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [t1].[Id], [t1].[CityId], [t1].[CreatedDate], [t1].[TourId], [c].[Id] AS [Id0], [c].[CountryId], [c].[CreatedDate] AS [CreatedDate0], [c].[Name], [c0].[Id] AS [Id1], [c0].[CreatedDate] AS [CreatedDate1], [c0].[Name] AS [Name0]
    FROM [TourCities] AS [t1]
    INNER JOIN [Cities] AS [c] ON [t1].[CityId] = [c].[Id]
    INNER JOIN [Countries] AS [c0] ON [c].[CountryId] = [c0].[Id]
) AS [t0] ON [t].[Id] = [t0].[TourId]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [t3].[Id], [t3].[ActivityId], [t3].[CreatedDate], [t3].[TourId], [a].[Id] AS [Id0], [a].[CreatedDate] AS [CreatedDate0], [a].[Name]
    FROM [TourActivities] AS [t3]
    INNER JOIN [Activities] AS [a] ON [t3].[ActivityId] = [a].[Id]

LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [t1].[Id], [t1].[CityId], [t1].[CreatedDate], [t1].[TourId], [c].[Id] AS [Id0], [c].[CountryId], [c].[CreatedDate] AS [CreatedDate0], [c].[Name], [c0].[Id] AS [Id1], [c0].[CreatedDate] AS [CreatedDate1], [c0].[Name] AS [Name0]

    INNER JOIN [Cities] AS [c] ON [t1].[CityId] = [c].[Id]
    INNER JOIN [Countries] AS [c0] ON [c].[CountryId] = [c0].[Id]
) AS [t0] ON [t].[Id] = [t0].[TourId]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [t3].[Id], [t3].[ActivityId], [t3].[CreatedDate], [t3].[TourId], [a].[Id] AS [Id0], [a].[CreatedDate] AS [CreatedDate0], [a].[Name]
